***manier.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:manier.html>manier</a> (392)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">maniere</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">maniere</i>. <span class="maintenance-line"><i>This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> incomplete. You can help Wiktionary by elaborating on the origins of this term.</i></span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:manier.html>manier</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:manieren.html>manieren</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:maniertje.html>maniertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>way, manner
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>Op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:manier.html>manier</a></i>  |  In that manner</dd></dl></li>

***manometer.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:manometer.html>manometer</a> (81592)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">manomètre</i>, formed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">μανός</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">manós</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">thin, <a href = vnd.unilang:rare.html>rare</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">μέτρον</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">métron</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:manometer.html>manometer</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:manometers.html>manometers</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>An instrument to measure pressure in a fluid, especially a double-legged liquid column gauge used to measure the difference in the pressures of two fluids.
<ul><li><b>1872</b>, <i>The American Journal of Science</i>
<dl><dd>As soon as the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:manometer.html>manometer</a></b> of the pump indicated the maximum of rarification, the apparatus <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> inclined <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span></dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1973</b>, Thomas Pynchon, <i>Gravity’s Rainbow</i>:
<dl><dd>Pökler helped in working out the Halbmodelle solution: bisecting the model lengthwise and mounting it flat-side to the wall of the test chamber, bringing the <a href = vnd.unilang:tubes.html>tubes</a> through that way to all the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:manometers.html>manometers</a></b> outside.</dd></dl></li></ul>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">manoscope</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">pressure gauge</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:manometer.html>manometer</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:meetinstrument.html>meetinstrument</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:waarmee.html>waarmee</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:druk.html>druk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wordt.html>wordt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gemeten.html>gemeten</a>.

***mantel.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:mantel.html>mantel</a> (8369)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:mantel.html>mantel</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">mantēllum</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mantel.html>mantel</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mantels.html>mantels</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mantel.html>manteltje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>cape, cloak, <a href = vnd.unilang:mantle.html>mantle</a></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">somewhat  dated  outside certain compounds</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> coat, jacket</li>
<li>surface (literal), lack of substance (figurative) <span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(<span id="rfv-sense-notice-nl-"></span>Can <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> verify<sup class="plainlinks">(<a class="external text" href="https://en.wiktionary.org/w/index.php?title=Wiktionary:Requests_for_verification/Non-Englishamp;action=editamp;section=newamp;preload=Template:rfv-sense/preloadamp;preloadtitle=%5B%5Bmantel%23rfv-sense-notice-nl-%7cmantel%5D%5D">+</a>)</sup> this sense?)</span></li></ol>

***mantle.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:mantle.html>mantle</a> (29209)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:mantel.html>mantel</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">mæntel</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">mentel</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">sleeveless cloak</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*mantil</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*mantilaz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:mantle.html>mantle</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; <a href = vnd.unilang:later.html>later</a> reinforced by <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Anglo-Norman_language" class="extiw" title="w:Anglo-Norman language">Anglo-Norman</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro"><a href = vnd.unilang:mantel.html>mantel</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">mantēllum</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">covering, cloak</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, diminutive of <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">mantum</i> (<span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">manteau</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Spanish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Spanish language">Spanish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="es">manto</i>), probably from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gaulish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Gaulish language">Gaulish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="cel-gau">*mantos</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="cel-gau">*mantalos</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">trodden road</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Celtic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Celtic language">Proto-Celtic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="cel-pro">*mantos</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="cel-pro">*mantlos</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*MenH-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">tread, press together; crumble</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:mantle.html>mantle</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">mantles</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A piece of clothing somewhat like an open robe or cloak, especially that worn by Orthodox <a href = vnd.unilang:bishops.html>bishops</a>. <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">Compare <i>mantum</i>.</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <span class="defdate">[from 9th c.]</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A figurative garment representing authority or status, capable of affording protection.
<dl><dd><i>At the meeting, she finally assumed the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:mantle.html>mantle</a></b> of leadership of the party.</i></dd>
<dd><i>The movement strove to put women under the protective <b><a href = vnd.unilang:mantle.html>mantle</a></b> of civil rights laws.</i></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Anything that <a href = vnd.unilang:covers.html>covers</a> or conceals something else; a cloak. <span class="defdate">[from 9th c.]</span>
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><i><abbr title="circa">c.</abbr></i> <b>1599-1602</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Shakespeare" class="extiw" title="w:William Shakespeare">William Shakespeare</a>,  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hamlet" class="extiw" title="w:Hamlet">The Tragedy of <a href = vnd.unilang:hamlet.html>Hamlet</a>, Prince of Denmark</a></cite>, Act 1, scene 1 |  republished as  <cite><a href = vnd.unilang:hamlet.html>Hamlet</a></cite>, New York |  Dover Publications, Inc., 1992, <small>→ISBN</small>, page 6:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">But look, the <a href = vnd.unilang:morn.html>morn</a>, in russet <b><a href = vnd.unilang:mantle.html>mantle</a></b> clad, walks <a href = vnd.unilang:o.html>o</a>'<a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>er</a> the dew of yon high eastward hill.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><i><abbr title="circa">c.</abbr></i> <b>1605-1606</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Shakespeare" class="extiw" title="w:William Shakespeare">William Shakespeare</a>,  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/King_Lear" class="extiw" title="w:King Lear">King Lear</a></cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">the green <b><a href = vnd.unilang:mantle.html>mantle</a></b> of the standing pool</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">malacology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The body wall of a mollusc, from which the shell <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> secreted. <span class="defdate">[from 15th c.]</span>
<ul><li><b>1990</b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:daniel.html>Daniel</a> L. <a href = vnd.unilang:gilbert.html>Gilbert</a>, William J. Adelman, John M. Arnold (<a href = vnd.unilang:editors.html>editors</a>), <i>Squid as Experimental Animals</i>, page 71:
<dl><dd>He grasps the female from slightly below about the mid-mantle region and positions himself so his arms are close to the opening of her <b><a href = vnd.unilang:mantle.html>mantle</a></b>.</dd></dl></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2017</b>,  Danna <a href = vnd.unilang:staaf.html>Staaf</a>,  <cite>Squid Empire</cite>, ForeEdge, <small>→ISBN</small>, page 8:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Molluscan <a href = vnd.unilang:bodies.html>bodies</a> are broadly divided into two parts: a muscular foot and a shell-secreting <b><a href = vnd.unilang:mantle.html>mantle</a></b>.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">ornithology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The back of a bird together with the folded wings.</li>
<li>The zone of hot gases around a flame.</li>
<li>A gauzy fabric impregnated with metal nitrates, used in some <a href = vnd.unilang:kinds.html>kinds</a> of gas and oil lamps and lanterns, which forms a rigid but fragile mesh of metal oxides when heated during initial use and then produces white light from the heat of the flame below it. <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">So called because it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> hung above the <a href = vnd.unilang:lamp.html>lamp</a>'s flame like a <i><a href = vnd.unilang:mantel.html>mantel</a></i>.</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <span class="defdate">[from 19th c.]</span></li>
<li>The outer wall and casing of a blast furnace, above the hearth.
<dl><dd><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Can <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> find and add a quotation of Raymond to this entry?)</span></dd></dl></li>
<li>A penstock for a water wheel.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">anatomy</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The cerebral cortex. <span class="defdate">[from 19th c.]</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">geology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The layer between the Earth's core and crust. <span class="defdate">[from 20th c.]</span></li>
<li>A fireplace shelf; <span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">Alternative spelling of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:mantel.html>mantel</a></i></span></span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">heraldry</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A mantling.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:mantle.html>mantle</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">mantles</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">mantling</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">mantled</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To cover or conceal (something); to cloak; to disguise.
<ul><li><b>1610-11</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Shakespeare" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:William Shakespeare">William Shakespeare</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Tempest" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:The Tempest">The Tempest</a></i>, Act V, Scene I
<dl><dd>As the morning <a href = vnd.unilang:steals.html>steals</a> upon the night, Melting the darkness; so their <a href = vnd.unilang:rising.html>rising</a> senses Begin to chace the ign'rant fumes, that <b><a href = vnd.unilang:mantle.html>mantle</a></b> Their clearer reason.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1610-11</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Shakespeare" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:William Shakespeare">William Shakespeare</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Tempest" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:The Tempest">The Tempest</a></i>, Act IV, Scene I
<dl><dd>I left them I' th' filthy <b>mantled</b> pool beyond your cell, There dancing up to th' chins.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To become covered or concealed. <span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Can <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> add an example for this sense?)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To spread like a <a href = vnd.unilang:mantle.html>mantle</a> (especially of blood in the face and cheeks when a person flushes).
<ul><li><b>1913</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/D.H._Lawrence" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:D.H. Lawrence">D.H. Lawrence</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sons_and_Lovers" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Sons and Lovers">Sons and <a href = vnd.unilang:lovers.html>Lovers</a></a></i>, <a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/Sons_and_Lovers/Chapter_10" class="extiw" title="s:Sons and Lovers/Chapter 10">chapter 10</a>
<dl><dd>The blood still <b>mantled</b> below her ears; she <a href = vnd.unilang:bent.html>bent</a> her head in shame of her humility.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
</body>

***manuele.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:manuele.html>manuele</a> (53922)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:manuele.html>manuele</a></strong>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:marbles.html>marbles</a> (41959)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:marbles.html>marbles</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="plural number">pl</abbr></span> (<i>plural only</i>)

<ol><li>Any of several children's games played with small glass <a href = vnd.unilang:balls.html>balls</a>.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">Egyptian boys played <b><a href = vnd.unilang:marbles.html>marbles</a></b> before the days of Moses.</i></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively<span class="ib-comma">,</span> usually in a limited number of expressions</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Sanity.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <i>see</i> Thesaurus:<span class="Latn" lang="en">sanity</span></span></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">Grandpa's <a href = vnd.unilang:lost.html>lost</a> his <b><a href = vnd.unilang:marbles.html>marbles</a></b>, but at least he still recognizes us.</i></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">Granny's still got all her <b><a href = vnd.unilang:marbles.html>marbles</a></b>.</i></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">His lack of <b><a href = vnd.unilang:marbles.html>marbles</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> becoming ever more apparent.</i></div></dd></dl>
<ul><li><b>2012</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/J._T._Petty" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:J. T. Petty">J. <a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>T</a>. Petty</a>, <i>Bloody Chester</i>, First Second, →ISBN, p. 63:
<dl><dd>—Her daddy's crazy. [...] Think she's <a href = vnd.unilang:looking.html>looking</a> for something? <br />—Treasure, I expect. That or maybe her daddy's <b><a href = vnd.unilang:marbles.html>marbles</a></b>.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>

<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2014</b>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:amen.html>Amen</a> Zwa,  <cite>Going Nowhere Fast In Assetto Corsa (2015-05-01)</cite>, <small>→ISBN</small>, page 395:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Some <a href = vnd.unilang:corners.html>corners</a> are littered with <b><a href = vnd.unilang:marbles.html>marbles</a></b>, off the racing line.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>

***marchanderen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:marchanderen.html>marchanderen</a> (81587)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">marchander</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:marchanderen.html>marchanderen</a></strong>
</p>

***marginaal.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:marginaal.html>marginaal</a> (68850)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">marginal</i>, from medieval <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">marginalis</i>, itself from Latin <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:margo.html>margo</a></i> 'edge' (from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*mereg-</i> "edge, boundary") + <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">-alis</i> '-al'
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:marginaal.html>marginaal</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:marginaal.html>marginaler</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">marginaalst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">literally</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> marginal, in or at the margin or edge(s)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figurative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> at the edge; borderline; destitute</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figurative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> socially <a href = vnd.unilang:outcast.html>outcast</a></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figurative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> (almost) insignificant, of minor importance</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">marginaliseren</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:marginaal.html>marginaal</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>marginally, slightly</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:marginaal.html>marginaal</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:marginalen.html>marginalen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:marginaal.html>marginaaltje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A marginal person, an <a href = vnd.unilang:outcast.html>outcast</a></li>
